ADDITIONAL NOTES
A. NOTES
Precipitation utiIized during winter months to meet forage freshwater requirements.
Irrigation weIls VCR DW 3, 12, 23, 25, & 30 were non-operational in 2023. AIl weIls wiIl be sampIed once the weIls become operational and used during the
cropping season. Heavy rains during the winter season aIlowed for a greater amount of surface water aIlocation to grow crops.
FieIds 23W Winter Forage, 1CCF Winter Forage, 2CCF Winter Forage, 3CCF Winter Forage, 12 AIfaIfa/Grass Mix, 15 AIfaIfa/Grass Mix, 16 AIfaIfa/Grass Mix,
21 AIfaIfa/Grass Mix, 5CCF AImonds, 7CCF AImonds, 10CCF AImonds, 11CCF AImonds, 12CCF AImonds, & 14CCF AImonds had lower than anticipated
removal rates. This was due to lower than expected N. The N was based on anaIysis that was derived through a certified laboratory. However, the
appIications to these fieIds matched the low removal rates and was abIe to meet the fieId ratio threshoId of 1.4.
FieIds 1CCFH Winter Forage, 2CCFH Winter Forage, 3CCFH Winter Forage, 4CCFH Winter Forage, 1CCF Corn, 3CCF Corn, 1CCFH Corn, & 14 Grass BIend
(TEFT) had lower than anticipated removal rates. This was due to lower than expected yieIds and expected N. The N was based on anaIysis that was
derived through a certified laboratory. However, the appIications to these fieIds matched the low removal rates and was abIe to meet the fieId ratio threshoId of
1.4.
FieIds 6CCF AImonds, 8CCF AImonds, 9CCF AImonds, & 13CCF AImonds had lower a than anticipated removal rates, which was due to low tonnage and N.
This resuIted in fieId ratios sIightIy exceeding target limits.
Nutrients appIied to permanent crops, such as trees and vines, are used for tree growth, vine deveIopment and fruit production (grapes, nuts, etc.). Comparing
nutrient appIications to nutrient content of harvested material for permanent crops is not appropriate and wiIl resuIt in high fieId ratios. A more accurate reporting
methodoIogy wiIl need to be deveIoped in order to account for nutrients retained in the permanent crops. AIl appIications wiIl continue to be monitored cIoseIy to
ensure that over appIication of nutrients does not occur.
FieIds 3 AIfaIfa, 6 AIfaIfa, 19 AIfaIfa, 20 AIfaIfa, 5CCF AImonds, 6CCF AImonds, 7CCF AImonds, 8CCF AImonds, 9CCF AImonds, 10CCF AImonds, 11CCF
AImonds, 12CCF AImonds, 13CCF AImonds, & 14CCF AImonds received no wastewater or soIid manure in 2023. AIl nutrients appIied to these fieIds were
contributed through freshwater appIications and/or commercial fertiIizer onIy.
FieId 11 was faIlow during the 2023 cropping season. FieId 15 was faIlow during the summer crop 2023.
